Statement Coverage for instance /\sb_tb_top#dut /u_sb_tx_init --

    Line         Item                      Count     Source 
    ----         ----                      -----     ------ 
  File ../../../Sideband/ucie_sb_tx_path.sv
    1                                                module ucie_sb_tx_path (

    2                                                

    3                                                    input logic i_clk,    // System / Control Clock

    4                                                    input logic i_s_clk,  // SerDes Clock  — pattern generation & output

    5                                                    input logic i_reset,  // Active-high asynchronous reset

    6                                                

    7                                                    // Control inputs

    8                                                    input logic i_sb_init_start,  // High during sideband initialisation

    9                                                    input logic i_timer_1ms,      // Pulse every 1 ms (from Timer module)

    10                                                   input logic i_rx_done,        // From RX path — pattern detected

    11                                               

    12                                                   // Physical outputs  (registered on i_s_clk)

    13                                                   output logic o_tx_sb_data,

    14                                                   output logic o_tx_sb_clk,

    15                                               

    16                                                   // Control output  (combinational from i_clk domain

    17                                                   output logic o_stop  // High when initialisation is fully done

    18                                               

    19                                               );

    20                                               

    21                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    22                                                 // Internal States & Counters

    23                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    24                                                 localparam IDLE = 2'b00;

    25                                                 localparam CYCLING = 2'b01;  // Alternating 1ms ON / 1ms OFF

    26                                                 localparam EXTRA_ITERS = 2'b10;  // Sending final 4 iterations

    27                                                 localparam DONE = 2'b11;  // Initialization complete

    28                                               

    29                                                 logic [1:0] current_state, next_state, current_state_serdes;

    30                                               

    31                                                 // Pattern Counters

    32                                                 // Total pattern length = 64 UI (Clk) + 32 UI (Low) = 96 UI

    33                                                 logic [6:0] ui_counter;  // Counter 0 to 95

    34                                                 logic [2:0] iter_counter;  // Counter 0 to 4 (for the extra iterations)

    35                                               

    36                                                 // 1ms Toggle Logic

    37                                                 logic       r_1ms_active;  // 1: Generating, 0: Quiet (swaps every 1ms)

    38                                                 logic       r_1ms_active_serdes;

    39                                               

    40                                                 // Generated Signals

    41                                                 logic       w_gen_data;

    42                                                 logic       w_gen_clk;

    43                                                 logic       w_pattern_running;  // High when we are actually shifting bits out

    44                                               

    45                                                 logic       r_clk_en_safe;

    46                                               

    47                                                 // Used to account for the time differences btw the slow clock and fast clock 

    48                                                 // since when detection is done and ui_counter reaches 95 and rx_done is asserted 

    49                                                 // we should go to Extra Iter state but we need to wait for the slow clock edge to come

    50                                                 // and between that the ui counter might move to 0 again to start next iterations before 

    51                                                 // the slow clock edge come --- That is why we need a flag to remeber this scene

    52                                                 logic       latch_flag;

    53                                               

    54                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    55                                                 // 1ms Alternating Logic

    56                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    57              1                       2786       always_ff @(posedge i_clk or posedge i_reset) begin

    58                                                   if (i_reset) begin

    59              1                        270           r_1ms_active <= 1'b1;  // Start active

    60                                                   end else if (current_state == IDLE) begin

    61              1                       1518           r_1ms_active <= 1'b1;

    62                                                   end else if (i_timer_1ms && (current_state == CYCLING || current_state == EXTRA_ITERS)) begin

    63              1                        324           r_1ms_active <= ~r_1ms_active;  // Toggle every 1ms

    64                                                   end

    65                                                 end

    66                                               

    67                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    68                                                 // Main FSM

    69                                                 // --------------------------------------------------------

    70              1                       1320       always_ff @(posedge i_clk or posedge i_reset) begin

    71                                                   if (i_reset) begin

    72              1                        240           current_state <= IDLE;

    73                                                   end else begin

    74              1                       1080           current_state <= next_state;

    75                                                   end

    76                                                 end

    77                                               

    78              1                     164976       always_ff @(posedge i_s_clk or posedge i_reset) begin

    79                                                   if (i_reset) begin

    80              1                        240           latch_flag <= 0;

    81                                                   end else begin

    82              1                    ***0***           if (ui_counter == 95 && i_rx_done && current_state == CYCLING) latch_flag <= 1;

    83              1                      46680           else if (current_state != CYCLING) latch_flag <= 0;

    84                                                   end

    85                                                 end

    86                                               

    87              1                     165366       always_comb begin

    88              1                     165366         next_state = current_state;

    89                                               

    90                                                   case (current_state)

    91                                                     IDLE: begin

    93                                                     end

    94

    98                                                       end

    139                                                    end

    140

    146                                                  end

    147                                                end

    148                                              

    149                                                // Sample it on the NEGEDGE so it is stable during the POSEDGE

    267                                              

    268                                                //---- SEQUENTIAL PROCESSES --------------------------------------------------

    269             1                     370499     always @(posedge i_clk or posedge i_reset) begin

    270                                                  if (i_reset) begin

    271             1                        240           o_req           <= 1'b0;

    272             1                        240           o_resp          <= 1'b0;

    273             1                        240           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    274             1                        240           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    275             1                        240           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    276             1                        240           o_valid         <= 1'b0;

    277             1                        240           stall_flag      <= 1'b0;

    278                                                  end

    279                                                  else begin

    280                                                  if (i_done || invalid_dec) begin

    281             1                     160724           stall_flag      <= 1'b0; // Clear stall flag on done signal

    282             1                     160724           o_req           <= 1'b0;

    283             1                     160724           o_resp          <= 1'b0;

    284             1                     160724           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    285             1                     160724           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    286             1                     160724           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    287             1                     160724           o_valid         <= 1'b0;

    288                                                  end

    289                                              

    290                                                  else if (!i_empty && !stall_flag) begin

    291             1                      84080           o_valid         <= dec_valid; // Valid message

    292             1                      84080           o_info_out      <= o_info_out_w; // Extract info field from input message

    293             1                      84080           o_data_out      <= o_data_out_w; // Extract data field from input message

    294             1                      84080           o_req           <= dec_req;

    295             1                      84080           o_resp          <= dec_resp;

    296             1                      84080           o_decoding      <= dec_decoding;

    297             1                      84080           stall_flag      <= 1'b1; // Mark that first message has been processed

    298                                                  end

    299                                                  else if (stall_flag)begin

    300             1                      42026           o_req           <= o_req;

    301             1                      42026           o_resp          <= o_resp;

    302             1                      42026           o_info_out      <= o_info_out;

    303             1                      42026           o_data_out      <= o_data_out;

    304             1                      42026           o_decoding      <= o_decoding;

    305             1                      42026           o_valid         <= o_valid;

    306                                                  end

    307                                                  else begin

    308             1                      83429           o_req           <= 1'b0;

    309             1                      83429           o_resp          <= 1'b0;

    310             1                      83429           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    311             1                      83429           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    312             1                      83429           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};

    313             1                      83429           o_valid         <= 1'b0;

    314                                                  end

    315                                                  end

    316                                                end // Decoding_proc

    317                                              

    318                                              

    319                                              

    320                                                //---- COMBINATIONAL LOGIC ---------------------------------------------------

    321                                              

    322                                              // ========== Combinational Decode ==========

    323                                              

    324                                              // --- Combinational parity and field extraction ---

    325                                              assign dec_msg_code    = i_msg_in[117:110];

    326                                              assign dec_msg_subcode = i_msg_in[71:64];

    327                                              assign dec_op_code     = i_msg_in[100:96];

    328                                              assign dec_srcid       = i_msg_in[127:125];

    329                                              assign dec_dstid       = i_msg_in[90:88];

    330             1                      30526     assign dec_dp          = ^{i_msg_in[63:0]};

    331             1                     222880     assign dec_cp          = ^{{i_msg_in[127:96], i_msg_in[93:64]}};

    332                                              

    333             1                     335229     assign dec_valid       = (invalid_dec) ? 1'b0 : ((dec_cp == i_msg_in[94]) && (dec_dp == i_msg_in[95]));

    334                                              

    335             1                     391232     assign o_dec_ready = !i_empty && !stall_flag;

    336             1                     315660     assign o_info_out_w =  (invalid_dec) ? {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}} : i_msg_in[87:72];

    337             1                     127006     assign o_data_out_w = (invalid_dec) ? {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}} : i_msg_in[63:0];

    338                                              

    339                                              // --- Combinational case decode ---

    340             1                     219704     always @(*) begin

    341             1                     219704       dec_req      = 1'b0;

    342             1                     219704       dec_resp     = 1'b0;

    343             1                     219704       invalid_dec  = 1'b0;

    344             1                     219704       dec_decoding = DEFAULT;

    345

    289                                                DEFAULT                            = {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}}
    290                                              } decoding_r;
    291                                              
    292                                              
    293                                              
    294                                                //---- SEQUENTIAL PROCESSES --------------------------------------------------
    295                                                //Decoding process
    296             1                     379585       always @(posedge i_clk or posedge i_reset) begin
    297                                                  if (i_reset) begin
    298             1                        240           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    299             1                        240           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    300             1                        240           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    301             1                        240           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    302             1                        240           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    303             1                        240           o_valid         <= 1'b0;
    304             1                        240           stall_flag      <= 1'b0;
    305                                                  end
    306                                                  else begin
    307                                                  if (i_done || invalid_dec) begin
    308             1                     160348           stall_flag      <= 1'b0; // Clear stall flag on done signal
    309             1                     160348           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    310             1                     160348           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    311             1                     160348           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    312             1                     160348           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    313             1                     160348           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    314             1                     160348           o_valid         <= 1'b0;
    315                                                  end
    316                                              
    317                                                  else if (!i_empty && !stall_flag) begin
    318             1                      87264           o_valid         <= dec_valid; // Valid message
    319             1                      87264           o_info_out      <= o_info_out_w; // Extract info field from input message
    320             1                      87264           o_data_out      <= o_data_out_w; // Extract data field from input message
    321             1                      87264           o_req           <= dec_req;
    322             1                      87264           o_resp          <= dec_resp;
    323             1                      87264           o_decoding      <= dec_decoding;
    324             1                      87264           stall_flag      <= 1'b1; // Mark that first message has been processed
    325                                                  end
    326                                                  else if (stall_flag)begin
    327             1                      44743           o_req           <= o_req;
    328             1                      44743           o_resp          <= o_resp;
    329             1                      44743           o_info_out      <= o_info_out;
    330             1                      44743           o_data_out      <= o_data_out;
    331             1                      44743           o_decoding      <= o_decoding;
    332             1                      44743           o_valid         <= o_valid;
    333                                                  end
    334                                                  else begin
    335             1                      86990           o_req           <= 1'b0;
    336             1                      86990           o_resp          <= 1'b0;
    337             1                      86990           o_info_out      <= {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    338             1                      86990           o_data_out      <= {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    339             1                      86990           o_decoding      <= {pDECODING_WIDTH{1'b0}};
    340             1                      86990           o_valid         <= 1'b0;
    341                                                  end
    342                                                  end
    343                                                end // Decoding_proc
    344                                              
    345                                              
    346                                                //---- COMBINATIONAL LOGIC ---------------------------------------------------
    347                                              // --- Combinational parity and field extraction ---
    348                                              assign dec_msg_code    = i_msg_in[117:110];
    349                                              assign dec_msg_subcode = i_msg_in[71:64];
    350                                              assign dec_op_code     = i_msg_in[100:96];
    351                                              assign dec_srcid       = i_msg_in[127:125];
    352                                              assign dec_dstid       = i_msg_in[90:88];
    353             1                      57013     assign dec_dp          = ^{i_msg_in[63:0]};
    354             1                     226826     assign dec_cp          = ^{{i_msg_in[127:96], i_msg_in[93:64]}};
    355                                              
    356             1                     345956     assign dec_valid       = (invalid_dec) ? 1'b0 : ((dec_cp == i_msg_in[94]) && (dec_dp == i_msg_in[95]));
    357                                              
    358             1                     401388     assign o_dec_ready = !i_empty && !stall_flag;
    359             1                     314439     assign o_info_out_w =  (invalid_dec) ? {pINFO_WIDTH{1'b0}} : i_msg_in[87:72];
    360             1                     149143     assign o_data_out_w = (invalid_dec) ? {pDATA_WIDTH{1'b0}} : i_msg_in[63:0];
    361                                              
    362                                              // --- Combinational case decode ---
    363             1                     223857     always @(*) begin
    364             1                     223857       dec_req      = 1'b0;
    365             1                     223857       dec_resp     = 1'b0;
    366             1                     223857       invalid_dec  = 1'b0;
